# High-Confidence Bivalent Domain Genes
# Source: Court & Arnaud (2017) Oncotarget 8(3):4110-4124
# PMID: 27926534 | PMC5354816
# DOI: 10.18632/oncotarget.14283
# Supplementary Table S8 (HC bivalent sheet): oncotarget-08-4110-s008.xlsx
#
# Bivalent chromatin domains carry both H3K4me3 (active) and H3K27me3 (repressive) marks.
# These 5,766 high-confidence (HC) bivalent regions were identified as present in
# ALL 5 human embryonic stem cell (hESC) lines analyzed (H1, H9, HUES1, HUES48, HUES64).
#
# Total HC bivalent regions: 5766
# Unique gene symbols: 5377
# Intergenic regions (no gene): 849
# Note: Some Excel date-converted gene names (SEPT genes) were restored.
#
